\DoxyCodeLine{00577\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ public\ domain\ branchless\ UTF-\/8\ decoder\ by\ Christopher\ Wellons:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00578\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ https://github.com/skeeto/branchless-\/utf8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00579\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Decode\ the\ next\ character,\ c,\ from\ s,\ reporting\ errors\ in\ e.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00580\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00581\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Since\ this\ is\ a\ branchless\ decoder,\ four\ bytes\ will\ be\ read\ from\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00582\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ buffer\ regardless\ of\ the\ actual\ length\ of\ the\ next\ character.\ This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00583\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ means\ the\ buffer\ \_must\_\ have\ at\ least\ three\ bytes\ of\ zero\ padding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00584\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ following\ the\ end\ of\ the\ data\ stream.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00585\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00586\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Errors\ are\ reported\ in\ e,\ which\ will\ be\ non-\/zero\ if\ the\ parsed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00587\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ character\ was\ somehow\ invalid:\ invalid\ byte\ sequence,\ non-\/canonical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00588\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ encoding,\ or\ a\ surrogate\ half.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00589\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00590\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ function\ returns\ a\ pointer\ to\ the\ next\ character.\ When\ an\ error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00591\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ occurs,\ this\ pointer\ will\ be\ a\ guess\ that\ depends\ on\ the\ particular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00592\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ error,\ but\ it\ will\ always\ advance\ at\ least\ one\ byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00593\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00594\ FMT\_CONSTEXPR\ \textcolor{keyword}{inline}\ \textcolor{keyword}{auto}\ utf8\_decode(\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*\ s,\ uint32\_t*\ c,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}*\ e)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00595\ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{00610\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Assume\ a\ four-\/byte\ character\ and\ load\ four\ bytes.\ Unused\ bits\ are}}
